# J

[Back to index](index.md)

## jab

### Sense 1: lexicon

- **Pronunciation:** `JAB`
- **Part of speech:** verb
- **Definition:** to bird, fly, or move as winged life
- **Register/status:** plain; accepted
- **Domains:** nature-ecology, travel-place, science-math
- **Root family:** `JB`; Nature; bird, winged creature, sky life; bird, winged creature, sky-moving life
- **Pattern:** verb
- **Literal:** J-B root, action vowel a
- **Example:** Na jab.
- **Corpus:** unattested (0 attestations)

## jab-da

- **Register/status:** plain; accepted

- **Pattern:** doctrine
- **Literal:** J-R-N root, doctrine suffix -lek
- **Example:** Jaran-lek lek e rih.
